## TOPIC 02251: Adjust9250(string, double)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-adjust9250__string-double.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-adjust9250__string-double.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Adjusts the external calibration constants for an NI 9250 device. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic void Adjust9250(string physicalChannels, double value)RemarksRefer to the calibration procedure for your device for detailed calibration instructions.After you commit the calibration, y

### Adjust9250(string, double)

Adjusts the [external calibration](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_calibration) constants for an NI 9250 device.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void Adjust9250(string physicalChannels, double value)

#### Remarks

Refer to the [calibration procedure for your device](https://#) for detailed calibration instructions.

Note

After you commit the calibration, you cannot undo it. If any calibration settings are incorrect, you must recalibrate the device.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| physicalChannels | string | The physical channel(s) to calibrate. |
| value | double | The reference value measured using a calibrator. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

ExternalCalibrationSession Class

## TOPIC 02263: Adjust9775(string, double, CalibrationCoupling9775)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-adjust9775__string-double-calibrationcoupling9775.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-adjust9775__string-double-calibrationcoupling9775.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Adjusts the external calibration constants for an NI 9775 device. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic void Adjust9775(string physicalChannels, double value, CalibrationCoupling9775 coupling)RemarksRefer to the calibration procedure for your device for detailed calibration instructions.A

### Adjust9775(string, double, CalibrationCoupling9775)

Adjusts the [external calibration](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_calibration) constants for an NI 9775 device.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void Adjust9775(string physicalChannels, double value, CalibrationCoupling9775 coupling)

#### Remarks

Refer to the [calibration procedure for your device](https://#) for detailed calibration instructions.

Note

After you commit the calibration, you cannot undo it. If any calibration settings are incorrect, you must recalibrate the device.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| physicalChannels | string | The physical channel(s) to calibrate. |
| value | double | The reference value measured using a calibrator. |
| coupling | CalibrationCoupling9775 | The coupling of the calibration constants to be adjusted. For more information, see CalibrationCoupling9775. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

ExternalCalibrationSession Class

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref path=nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-adjustaoseries__double.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 02264: AdjustAOSeries(double)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-adjustaoseries__double.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-adjustaoseries__double.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Adjusts the external calibration constants on an AO Series device. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic void AdjustAOSeries(double referenceVoltage)RemarksYou must connect a known voltage to the device and specify that voltage with referenceVoltage .ParametersNameTypeDescriptionreference

### AdjustAOSeries(double)

Adjusts the [external calibration](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_devcalibrate) constants on an AO Series device.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void AdjustAOSeries(double referenceVoltage)

#### Remarks

You must [connect a known voltage to the device](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxdevconsid_calsigaoseries) and specify that voltage with *referenceVoltage* .

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| referenceVoltage | double | The known voltage to use as a reference for calibration. This voltage must be between +6.000 V and +9.999 V. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

ExternalCalibrationSession Class

### AdjustDsaAI(double, bool)

## TOPIC 02270: AdjustDsaAO(long, double, double, double, double, double)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-adjustdsaao__long-double-double-double-double-double.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-adjustdsaao__long-double-double-double-double-double.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Adjusts the external calibration constants for the analog output section of a DSA device. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic void AdjustDsaAO(long channel, double requestedLowVoltage, double actualLowVoltage, double requestedHighVoltage, double actualHighVoltage, double gainSetting)Rem

### AdjustDsaAO(long, double, double, double, double, double)

Adjusts the [external calibration](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_calibration) constants for the analog output section of a DSA device.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void AdjustDsaAO(long channel, double requestedLowVoltage, double actualLowVoltage, double requestedHighVoltage, double actualHighVoltage, double gainSetting)

#### Remarks

You must use the device to generate a high voltage and low voltage at a specified gain, measure the high and low voltages, then specify the requested high voltage, low voltage, and gain along with the actual high voltage and low voltage.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| channel | long | The number of the channel to calibrate. This number is the numeric portion of the physical channel name, not the full physical channel name. |
| requestedLowVoltage | double | The low voltage you attempted to generate at the gainSetting you specified. |
| actualLowVoltage | double | The actual low voltage as measured by an external sensor. |
| requestedHighVoltage | double | The high voltage you attempted to generate at the gainSetting you specified. |
| actualHighVoltage | double | The actual high voltage as measured by an external sensor. |
| gainSetting | double | The gain setting you used when you attempted to generate the requestedHighVoltage and requestedLowVoltage . |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

ExternalCalibrationSession Class

- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-adjustdsaaotimebase__double-out.html`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Adjusts the external calibration constants for the timebase of a DSA device with an adjustible oscillator. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic void AdjustDsaAOTimebase(double measuredFrequency, out bool calibrationComplete)RemarksYou must first call SetupDsaAOTimebase and measure the fr

### AdjustDsaAOTimebase(double, out bool)

Adjusts the [external calibration](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_calibration) constants for the timebase of a DSA device with an adjustible oscillator.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void AdjustDsaAOTimebase(double measuredFrequency, out bool calibrationComplete)

#### Remarks

You must first call [SetupDsaAOTimebase](nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-setupdsaaotimebase.html) and measure the frequency of the resulting sine wave. Repeat this process until *calibrationComplete*  returns true.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| measuredFrequency | double | The measured frequency of the sine wave generated by the device. |
| calibrationComplete | out bool | Returns true if calibration of the device is complete. If this parameter returns false, repeat the calibration process. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

ExternalCalibrationSession Class

Configures a connection on the SC Express accessory for the specified physical channel(s).

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void ConnectSCExpressCalibrationAccessoryChannels(string physicalChannels, string connection)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| physicalChannels | string | The physical channel(s) to calibrate. |
| connection | string | Specifies how channels on the SC Express accessory should be configured. The resulting configuration connects channels to a particular external signal or to an onboard terminal. The supported connections depend on the accessory. |

Parent topic:

ExternalCalibrationSession Class

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public double[] Get9775AdjustmentPoints(CalibrationCoupling9775 coupling)

#### Remarks

Refer to the [calibration procedure for your device](https://#) for detailed calibration instructions.

Note

After you commit the calibration, you cannot undo it. If any calibration settings are incorrect, you must recalibrate the device.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| coupling | CalibrationCoupling9775 | The coupling of the calibration constants to be adjusted. For more information, see CalibrationCoupling9775. |

#### Returns

A 1D array of reference values.

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

ExternalCalibrationSession Class

The terminal on which to measure module output depends on the configuration of the module in MAX. ### Setup11637(string, AIBridgeConfiguration11637, double)

Sets up external calibration for an FD 11637 device.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void Setup11637(string physicalChannels, AIBridgeConfiguration11637 bridgeConfiguration, double excitationValue)

#### Remarks

calibration procedure for your device

Note

After you commit the calibration, you cannot undo it. If any calibration settings are incorrect, you must recalibrate the device.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| physicalChannels | string | Specifies the name of the physical channel to use to create the virtual channel. The DAQmx physical channel constant lists all physical channels for devices installed in the system. You cannot specify more than one physical channel. |
| bridgeConfiguration | AIBridgeConfiguration11637 | The type of Wheatstone bridge the sensor is. |
| excitationValue | double | Specifies the excitation value for the current channel and bridge configuration. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

### Setup9219(string, double, double, AIMeasurementType, AIBridgeConfiguration)

Sets up external calibration for an NI 9219 device.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void Setup9219(string physicalChannels, double rangeMinimum, double rangeMaximum, AIMeasurementType measurementType, AIBridgeConfiguration bridgeConfiguration)

#### Remarks

calibration procedure for your device

Note

After you commit the calibration, you cannot undo it. If any calibration settings are incorrect, you must recalibrate the device.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| physicalChannels | string | Specifies the name of the physical channel to use to create the virtual channel. The DAQmx physical channel constant lists all physical channels for devices installed in the system. You cannot specify more than one physical channel. |
| rangeMinimum | double | The minimum value in the range, in the units of the measurement type specified by measurementType . If your measurementType is RTD, you must specify your minimum range in ohms. |
| rangeMaximum | double | The maximum value in the range, in the units of the measurement type specified by measurementType . If your measurementType is RTD, you must specify your maximum range in ohms. |
| measurementType | AIMeasurementType | The type of measurement for the device. |
| bridgeConfiguration | AIBridgeConfiguration | The type of Wheatstone bridge the sensor is. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

ExternalCalibrationSession Class

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-setup9269__string-int.html`

SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic void Setup9269(string physicalChannels, int value)RemarksRefer to the calibration procedu

### Setup9269(string, int)

Writes the specified binary value to the DAC on the specified physical channel. This method requires a sweep of DAC values obtained from [Get9269AdjustmentPoints](nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-get9269adjustmentpoints.html).

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void Setup9269(string physicalChannels, int value)

#### Remarks

calibration procedure for your device

Note

After you commit the calibration, you cannot undo it. If any calibration settings are incorrect, you must recalibrate the device.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| physicalChannels | string | Specifies the name of the physical channel to use to create the virtual channel. The DAQmx physical channel constant lists all physical channels for devices installed in the system. You cannot specify more than one physical channel. |
| value | int | The binary number to write to the DAC. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

### SetupDsaAOTimebase()

Generates a sine wave of a fixed frequency from the DSA device. You must measure the frequency of the generated sine wave and pass that value into [AdjustDsaAOTimebase(double, out bool)](nationalinstruments-daqmx-externalcalibrationsession-adjustdsaaotimebase__double-out.html).

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public double SetupDsaAOTimebase()

#### Remarks

calibration procedure for your device

Note

After you commit the calibration, you cannot undo it. If any calibration settings are incorrect, you must recalibrate the device.

#### Returns

The expected frequency of the sine wave of a calibrated device.

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

- source_description: Represents a handle to an external calibration session on a device. Derives fromMarshalByRefObjectIDisposableSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic class ExternalCalibrationSession : MarshalByRefObject, IDisposableRemarksExample applications are located in the <Public Documents>\National I

### ExternalCalibrationSession Class

Represents a handle to an [external calibration](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_devcalibrate) session on a device.

#### Derives from

- MarshalByRefObject
- IDisposable

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public class ExternalCalibrationSession : MarshalByRefObject, IDisposable

#### Remarks

Note

Example applications are located in the <*Public Documents*>\National Instruments\NI-DAQ\Examples\DotNET4.*x* directory or in the **Start** menu at **National Instruments»NI-DAQmx»NI-DAQmx Examples**.

Use [StartExternalCalibration(string)](nationalinstruments-daqmx-device-startexternalcalibration__string.html) to start an external calibration and create an instance of this class.

#### Thread Safety

All members of this type are safe for multithreaded operations.

## TOPIC 02404: ConfigureInterlockedTrigger(string, InterlockedHandshakeTriggerAssertedLevel)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-handshaketrigger-configureinterlockedtrigger__string-interlockedhandshaketriggerassertedlevel.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-handshaketrigger-configureinterlockedtrigger__string-interlockedhandshaketriggerassertedlevel.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Configures the task to stop the acquisition when the device acquires all pretrigger samples; an analog signal reaches the level you specify; and the device acquires all post-trigger samples. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic void ConfigureInterlockedTrigger(string source, InterlockedH

### ConfigureInterlockedTrigger(string, InterlockedHandshakeTriggerAssertedLevel)

Configures the task to stop the acquisition when the device acquires all pretrigger samples; an [analog signal reaches the level you specify](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_analogtriggering); and the device acquires all post-trigger samples.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void ConfigureInterlockedTrigger(string source, InterlockedHandshakeTriggerAssertedLevel assertedLevel)

#### Remarks

The NI-DAQmx driver does not determine if the requested settings are possible until the task is verified. ConfigureInterlockedTrigger(string, InterlockedHandshakeTriggerAssertedLevel) does not throw an exception for parameter values that are not compatible with your hardware or other settings in your task. To determine if all of the settings for a [Task](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task.html) are valid, you must verify the task by starting the task, either with [Start](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task-start.html) or by reading from or writing to the task, or by calling [Control(TaskAction)](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task-control__taskaction.html) with [Verify](nationalinstruments-daqmx-taskaction.html).

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| source | string | The name of a virtual channel or terminal where there is an analog signal to use as the source of the trigger. For E Series devices, if you use a virtual channel, it must be the only channel in the task. The only terminal you can use for E Series devices is PFI0. |
| assertedLevel | InterlockedHandshakeTriggerAssertedLevel | The value of the desired HandshakeEventInterlockedAssertedLevel. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

HandshakeTrigger Class

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref path=nationalinstruments-daqmx-handshaketrigger-configurenone.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 02405: ConfigureNone()

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-handshaketrigger-configurenone.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-handshaketrigger-configurenone.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Disables handshake triggering for the measurement. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic void ConfigureNone()RemarksThe NI-DAQmx driver does not determine if the requested settings are possible until the task is verified. ConfigureNone does not throw an exception for parameter values that

### ConfigureNone()

Disables [handshake triggering](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_handshaking) for the measurement.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void ConfigureNone()

#### Remarks

The NI-DAQmx driver does not determine if the requested settings are possible until the task is verified. [ConfigureNone](nationalinstruments-daqmx-referencetrigger-configurenone.html) does not throw an exception for parameter values that are not compatible with your hardware or other settings in your task. To determine if all of the settings for a [Task](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task.html) are valid, you must verify the task by starting the task, either with [Start](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task-start.html) or by reading from or writing to the task, or by calling [Control(TaskAction)](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task-control__taskaction.html) with [Verify](nationalinstruments-daqmx-taskaction.html).

#### Exceptions

## TOPIC 02409: HandshakeTrigger Class

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-handshaketrigger.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-handshaketrigger.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Contains properties and methods that configure handshake trigger signals on a task. Derives fromMarshalByRefObjectIFilteredTypeDescriptorSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic class HandshakeTrigger : MarshalByRefObject, IFilteredTypeDescriptorRemarksExample applications are located in the

### HandshakeTrigger Class

Contains properties and methods that configure [handshake trigger signals on a task](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_handshaking).

#### Derives from

- MarshalByRefObject
- IFilteredTypeDescriptor

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public class HandshakeTrigger : MarshalByRefObject, IFilteredTypeDescriptor

#### Remarks

Note

Example applications are located in the <*Public Documents*>\National Instruments\NI-DAQ\Examples\DotNET4.*x* directory or in the **Start** menu at **National Instruments»NI-DAQmx»NI-DAQmx Examples**.

#### Thread Safety

All members of this type are safe for multithreaded operations.

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Interlocked | Gets the InterlockedHandshakeTrigger. |
| Type | Specifies the type of Handshake Trigger to use. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ConfigureInterlockedTrigger(string, InterlockedHandshakeTriggerAssertedLevel) | Configures the task to stop the acquisition when the device acquires all pretrigger samples; an analog signal reaches the level you specify; and the device acquires all post-trigger samples. |
| ConfigureNone() | Disables handshake triggering for the measurement. |
| ToString() | Returns a string representation of the object. |

#### See Also

- Triggers
- HandshakeTrigger

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.DAQmx

## TOPIC 02412: GetFilteredTypeDescriptor(PropertyFilterType, PropertyFilterFlags)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-ifilteredtypedescriptor-getfilteredtypedescriptor__propertyfiltertype-propertyfilterflags.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-ifilteredtypedescriptor-getfilteredtypedescriptor__propertyfiltertype-propertyfilterflags.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Returns a list of filtered properties that belong to the Task subobject, according to the specified filtering type and filter flags. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic ICustomTypeDescriptor GetFilteredTypeDescriptor(PropertyFilterType filterType, PropertyFilterFlags filterFlags)Remarks

### GetFilteredTypeDescriptor(PropertyFilterType, PropertyFilterFlags)

Returns a list of filtered properties that belong to the [Task](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task.html) subobject, according to the specified filtering type and filter flags.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public ICustomTypeDescriptor GetFilteredTypeDescriptor(PropertyFilterType filterType, PropertyFilterFlags filterFlags)

#### Remarks

Property filtering is a mechanism whereby you can programmatically retrieve a list of properties that are applicable to a specific task's subobject, based on the filtering type.

You can call the Overload:System.ComponentModel.ICustomTypeDescriptor.GetProperties method on the returned ICustomTypeDescriptor in order to access the list of properties as a PropertyDescriptorCollection. When GetProperties(Attribute) is called with an attribute array as a filter, the returned properties are filtered as if they all have the BrowsableAttribute set to true.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| filterType | PropertyFilterType | The type of filtering to perform. |
| filterFlags | PropertyFilterFlags | The filtering options. |

#### Returns

An ICustomTypeDescriptor that contains the filtered properties.

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ArgumentException | An invalid enumeration value was passed as an argument to the function. |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

IFilteredTypeDescriptor Interface

### IFilteredTypeDescriptor Interface

Defines the interface that is implemented by all [Task](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task.html) subobjects that can perform property filtering by programmatically returning an ICustomTypeDescriptor that contains the list of filtered properties for the subobject.

#### Derives from

None

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public interface IFilteredTypeDescriptor

#### Remarks

- [AIChannel](nationalinstruments-daqmx-aichannel.html)
- [AnalogEdgeReferenceTrigger](nationalinstruments-daqmx-analogedgereferencetrigger.html)
- [AnalogEdgeStartTrigger](nationalinstruments-daqmx-analogedgestarttrigger.html)
- [AnalogLevelPauseTrigger](nationalinstruments-daqmx-analoglevelpausetrigger.html)
- [AnalogWindowPauseTrigger](nationalinstruments-daqmx-analogwindowpausetrigger.html)
- [AnalogWindowReferenceTrigger](nationalinstruments-daqmx-analogwindowreferencetrigger.html)
- [AnalogWindowStartTrigger](nationalinstruments-daqmx-analogwindowstarttrigger.html)
- [AOChannel](nationalinstruments-daqmx-aochannel.html)
- [ArmStartTrigger](nationalinstruments-daqmx-armstarttrigger.html)
- [CIChannel](nationalinstruments-daqmx-cichannel.html)
- [COChannel](nationalinstruments-daqmx-cochannel.html)
- [DaqBuffer](nationalinstruments-daqmx-daqbuffer.html)
- [DaqStream](nationalinstruments-daqmx-daqstream.html)
- [DIChannel](nationalinstruments-daqmx-dichannel.html)
- [DigitalEdgeAdvanceTrigger](nationalinstruments-daqmx-digitaledgeadvancetrigger.html)
- [DigitalEdgeArmStartTrigger](nationalinstruments-daqmx-digitaledgearmstarttrigger.html)
- [DigitalEdgeReferenceTrigger](nationalinstruments-daqmx-digitaledgereferencetrigger.html)
- [DigitalEdgeStartTrigger](nationalinstruments-daqmx-digitaledgestarttrigger.html)
- [DigitalEdgeWatchdogExpirationTrigger](nationalinstruments-daqmx-digitaledgewatchdogexpirationtrigger.html)

## TOPIC 02422: LinearScale(string, double, double)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-linearscale-linearscale__string-double-double.html`

- source_description: Initializes a new instance of the LinearScale class that scales values using the equation y = mx + b, where x is the prescaled value, and y is the scaled value. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic LinearScale(string name, double slope, double yIntercept)RemarksThe equation is identical

### LinearScale(string, double, double)

Initializes a new instance of the [LinearScale](nationalinstruments-daqmx-linearscale.html) class that scales values using the equation *y = mx + b*, where *x* is the prescaled value, and *y* is the scaled value.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public LinearScale(string name, double slope, double yIntercept)

#### Remarks

The equation is identical for input and output. If the equation is in the form *x = my + b*, you must first solve for *y* in terms of *x*.

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| name | string | The name of the custom scale for later use, such as when you create a virtual channel. |
| slope | double | The slope, m, in the equation. |
| yIntercept | double | The y-intercept, b, in the equation. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

LinearScale Class

## TOPIC 02426: LoggingMode Enumeration

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-loggingmode.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-loggingmode.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether to enable logging and whether to allow reading data while logging. Log mode allows for the best performance. However, you cannot read data while logging if you specify this mode. If you want to read data while logging, specify Log and Read mode. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments

### LoggingMode Enumeration

Specifies whether to enable [logging](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_datalogging) and whether to allow reading data while logging. Log mode allows for the best performance. However, you cannot read data while logging if you specify this mode. If you want to read data while logging, specify Log and Read mode.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public enum LoggingMode

#### Remarks

Specifies whether to enable [logging](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_datalogging) and whether to allow reading data while logging. Log mode allows for the best performance. However, you cannot read data while logging if you specify this mode. If you want to read data while logging, specify Log and Read mode. Use this enumeration to get or set the value of [LoggingMode](nationalinstruments-daqmx-daqstream-loggingmode.html).

#### Members

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Off | 10231 | Disable logging for the task. |
| Log | 15844 | Enable logging for the task. You cannot read data using reading from the task when using this mode. If you require access to the data, read from the TDMS file. |
| LogAndRead | 15842 | Enable both logging and reading data for the task. You must use reading from the task to read samples for NI-DAQmx to stream them to disk. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.DAQmx

## TOPIC 02430: ConfigureAnalogLevelTrigger(string, AnalogLevelPauseTriggerCondition, double)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-pausetrigger-configureanalogleveltrigger__string-analoglevelpausetriggercondition-double.html`

- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Configures the task to pause acquisition or generation when an analog signal is above or below a level you specify. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic void ConfigureAnalogLevelTrigger(string source, AnalogLevelPauseTriggerCondition condition, double level)RemarksThe NI-DAQmx driver doe

### ConfigureAnalogLevelTrigger(string, AnalogLevelPauseTriggerCondition, double)

Configures the task to pause acquisition or generation when an analog signal is [above or below a level you specify](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_analogtriggering).

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void ConfigureAnalogLevelTrigger(string source, AnalogLevelPauseTriggerCondition condition, double level)

#### Remarks

The NI-DAQmx driver does not determine if the requested settings are possible until the task is verified. ConfigureAnalogLevelTrigger(string, AnalogLevelPauseTriggerCondition, double) does not throw an exception for parameter values that are not compatible with your hardware or other settings in your task. To determine if all of the settings for a [Task](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task.html) are valid, you must verify the task by starting the task, either with [Start](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task-start.html) or by reading from or writing to the task, or by calling [Control(TaskAction)](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task-control__taskaction.html) with [Verify](nationalinstruments-daqmx-taskaction.html).

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| source | string | The name of a virtual channel or terminal where there is an analog signal to use as the source of the trigger. |
| condition | AnalogLevelPauseTriggerCondition | Specifies if the task pauses acquiring and generating samples when the signal is below level or above level . |
| level | double | The analog threshold level, in the units of the measurement or generation. Use condition to specify if the task pauses above or below this threshold. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

PauseTrigger Class

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-pausetrigger-configuredigitalpatterntrigger__string-string-digitalpatternpausetriggercondition.html`

SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic void ConfigureDigitalPatternTrigger(string source, string pattern, DigitalPatternPauseTriggerCondition condition)RemarksThe NI-DAQmx driver does not de

### ConfigureDigitalPatternTrigger(string, string, DigitalPatternPauseTriggerCondition)

Configures a task to pause the acquisition or generation when the device matches a [digital pattern](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_digpattern).

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void ConfigureDigitalPatternTrigger(string source, string pattern, DigitalPatternPauseTriggerCondition condition)

#### Remarks

The NI-DAQmx driver does not determine if the requested settings are possible until the task is verified. ConfigureDigitalPatternTrigger(string, string, DigitalPatternPauseTriggerCondition) does not throw an exception for parameter values that are not compatible with your hardware or other settings in your task. To determine if all of the settings for a [Task](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task.html) are valid, you must verify the task by starting the task. You start the task with [Start](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task-start.html), by reading from or writing to the task, or by calling [Control(TaskAction)](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task-control__taskaction.html) with [Verify](nationalinstruments-daqmx-taskaction.html).

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| source | string | The physical channels to use for pattern matching. The order of the physical channels determines the order of the pattern. If a port is included, the order of the physical channels within the port is in ascending order. |
| pattern | string | The digital pattern that must be met for the trigger to occur. |
| condition | DigitalPatternPauseTriggerCondition | The condition under which the trigger occurs. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref path=nationalinstruments-daqmx-pausetrigger-configurenone.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 02434: ConfigureNone()

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-pausetrigger-configurenone.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-pausetrigger-configurenone.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Disables pause triggering for the task. Once started, samples are acquired or generated until the requested number has been acquired or generated, or the task has stopped. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic void ConfigureNone()RemarksThe NI-DAQmx driver does not determine if the reques

### ConfigureNone()

Disables [pause triggering](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_pausetrigger) for the task. Once started, samples are acquired or generated until the requested number has been acquired or generated, or the task has stopped.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public void ConfigureNone()

#### Remarks

The NI-DAQmx driver does not determine if the requested settings are possible until the task is verified. ConfigureNone does not throw an exception for parameter values that are not compatible with your hardware or other settings in your task. To determine if all of the settings for a [Task](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task.html) are valid, you must verify the task by starting the task, either with [Start](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task-start.html) or by reading from or writing to the task, or by calling [Control(TaskAction)](nationalinstruments-daqmx-task-control__taskaction.html) with [Verify](nationalinstruments-daqmx-taskaction.html).

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

PauseTrigger Class

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref path=nationalinstruments-daqmx-pausetrigger.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 02440: PauseTrigger Class

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-pausetrigger.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-pausetrigger.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Contains properties and methods that configure signals and triggers that pause a task. Derives fromMarshalByRefObjectIFilteredTypeDescriptorSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic class PauseTrigger : MarshalByRefObject, IFilteredTypeDescriptorRemarksExample applications are located in the

### PauseTrigger Class

Contains properties and methods that configure [signals and triggers that pause a task](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_pausetrigger).

#### Derives from

- MarshalByRefObject
- IFilteredTypeDescriptor

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public class PauseTrigger : MarshalByRefObject, IFilteredTypeDescriptor

#### Remarks

Note

Example applications are located in the <*Public Documents*>\National Instruments\NI-DAQ\Examples\DotNET4.*x* directory or in the **Start** menu at **National Instruments»NI-DAQmx»NI-DAQmx Examples**.

#### Thread Safety

All members of this type are safe for multithreaded operations.

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| AnalogLevel | Gets the AnalogLevelPauseTrigger. |
| AnalogWindow | Gets the AnalogWindowPauseTrigger. |
| DigitalLevel | Gets the DigitalLevelPauseTrigger. |
| DigitalPattern | Gets the DigitalPatternPauseTrigger. |
| Terminal | Indicates the name of the internal Pause Trigger terminal for the task. This property does not return the name of the trigger source terminal. |
| Type | Specifies the type of trigger to use to pause a task. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ConfigureAnalogLevelTrigger(string, AnalogLevelPauseTriggerCondition, double) | Configures the task to pause acquisition or generation when an analog signal is above or below a level you specify. |
| ConfigureAnalogWindowTrigger(string, AnalogWindowPauseTriggerCondition, double, double) | Configures the task to pause acquisition or generation when an analog signal is inside or outside of a range you specify. |
| ConfigureDigitalLevelTrigger(string, DigitalLevelPauseTriggerCondition) | Configures the task to pause acquisition or generation based on the level of a digital signal. |
| ConfigureDigitalPatternTrigger(string, string, DigitalPatternPauseTriggerCondition) | Configures a task to pause the acquisition or generation when the device matches a digital pattern. |
| ConfigureNone() | Disables pause triggering for the task. Once started, samples are acquired or generated until the requested number has been acquired or generated, or the task has stopped. |
| ToString() | Returns a string representation of the object. |

#### See Also

- Triggers
- PauseTrigger

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.DAQmx

## TOPIC 02442: PauseTriggerType Enumeration

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-pausetriggertype.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-pausetriggertype.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the type of trigger to use to pause a task. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic enum PauseTriggerTypeRemarksSpecifies the type of trigger to use to pause a task. Use this enumeration to get or set the value of Type.MembersNameValueDescriptionAnalogLevel10101Pause the measureme

### PauseTriggerType Enumeration

Specifies the [type](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_analogtriggering) of trigger to use to pause a task.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public enum PauseTriggerType

#### Remarks

Specifies the [type](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_analogtriggering) of trigger to use to pause a task. Use this enumeration to get or set the value of [Type](nationalinstruments-daqmx-pausetrigger-type.html).

#### Members

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| AnalogLevel | 10101 | Pause the measurement or generation while an analog signal is above or below a level. |
| AnalogWindow | 10103 | Pause the measurement or generation while an analog signal is either inside or outside of a range of values. |
| DigitalLevel | 10152 | Pause the measurement or generation while a digital signal is at either a high or low state. |
| DigitalPattern | 10398 | Pause the measurement or generation while digital physical channels either match or do not match a digital pattern. |
| None | 10230 | Do not pause the measurement or generation. |

Parent topic:

NationalInstruments.DAQmx

### AIInputSources

Indicates the list of input sources supported by the channel. Channels may support using the signal from the I/O connector or one of several calibration signals.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public string[] AIInputSources { get; }

#### Remarks

This property returns a copy of the actual array. Avoid calling this property within a for loop because it creates a copy for each iteration of the loop. Avoid using an indexer to set a member of the array because the indexer returns a copy of the object and has no effect on the actual object.

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`

SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic bool AOPowerAmplifierChannelEnable { get; set; }ExceptionsTypeDescriptionNationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqExceptionThe NI-

### AOPowerAmplifierChannelEnable

Specifies whether to enable or disable a channel for amplification. This property can also be used to check if a channel is enabled.

#### Remarks

## TOPIC 02490: PhysicalChannel Class

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-physicalchannel.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-physicalchannel.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Encapsulates one or more channels on an NI-DAQmx device and contains functions and properties that operate on the channel outside the context of a task. Derives fromMarshalByRefObjectIDisposableSyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic class PhysicalChannel : MarshalByRefObject, IDisposableRe

### PhysicalChannel Class

Encapsulates one or more channels on an NI-DAQmx device and contains functions and properties that operate on the [channel](/csh?context=nidaqmx_mxcncpts_chans) outside the context of a task.

#### Derives from

- MarshalByRefObject
- IDisposable

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public class PhysicalChannel : MarshalByRefObject, IDisposable

#### Remarks

LoadPhysicalChannel(string)

Local

DaqSystem

Note

Example applications are located in the <*Public Documents*>\National Instruments\NI-DAQ\Examples\DotNET4.*x* directory or in the **Start** menu at **National Instruments»NI-DAQmx»NI-DAQmx Examples**.

#### Thread Safety

All members of this type are safe for multithreaded operations.

#### Properties

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| AIInputSources | Indicates the list of input sources supported by the channel. Channels may support using the signal from the I/O connector or one of several calibration signals. |
| AISupportedMeasurementTypes | Gets the measurement types supported by the physical channels of the device. |
| AITerminalConfigurations | Indicates the list of input terminal configurations supported by the channel. |
| AOManualControlAmplitude | Indicates the current value of the front panel amplitude control for the physical channel in volts. |
| AOManualControlEnable | Specifies if you can control the physical channel externally via a manual control located on the device. You cannot simultaneously control a channel manually and with NI-DAQmx. |
| AOManualControlFrequency | Indicates the current value of the front panel frequency control for the physical channel in hertz. |
| AOManualControlShortDetected | Indicates whether the physical channel is currently disabled due to a short detected on the channel. |
| AOPowerAmplifierChannelEnable | Specifies whether to enable or disable a channel for amplification. This property can also be used to check if a channel is enabled. |
| AOPowerAmplifierGain | Indicates the calibrated gain of the channel. |
| AOPowerAmplifierOffset | Indicates the calibrated offset of the channel in volts. |
| AOPowerAmplifierOvercurrent | Indicates if the channel detected an overcurrent condition. |
| AOPowerAmplifierScalingCoefficients | Indicates the coefficients of a polynomial equation used to scale from pre-amplified values. |
| AOSupportedOutputTypes | Gets the generation types supported by the physical channels of the device. |
| AOTerminalConfigurations | Indicates the list of output terminal configurations supported by the channel. |
| CISupportedMeasurementTypes | Gets the measurement types supported by the physical channels of the device. |
| COSupportedOutputTypes | Gets the generation types supported by the physical channels of the device. |
| DIChangeDetectionSupported | Indicates if the change detection timing type is supported for the digital input physical channel. |
| DigPortLogicFamily | Specifies the digital port logic family to use for acquisition and generation. A logic family corresponds to voltage thresholds that are compatible with a group of voltage standards. Refer to the device documentation for information on the logic high and logic low voltages for these logic families. |
| DIPortWidth | Indicates in bits the width of digital input port. |
| DISampleClockSupported | Indicates if the sample clock timing type is supported for the digital input physical channel. |
| DISampleModes | Gets the sample modes supported by the physical channels that support sample clocked digital input. |
| DOPortWidth | Indicates in bits the width of digital output port. |
| DOSampleClockSupported | Indicates if the sample clock timing type is supported for the digital output physical channel. |
| DOSampleModes | Gets the sample modes supported by physical channels that support sample clocked digital output. |
| PhysicalChannelName | Gets the name of the physical channel. |
| PowerControlEnable | Specifies whether to turn on the sensor's power supply. |
| PowerControlType | Specifies the type of power supplied to the sensor. |
| PowerControlVoltage | Specifies the voltage level for the sensor's power supply. |
| SensorPowerOpenChannel | Indicates whether there is an open channel or undercurrent condition on the channel. |
| SensorPowerOvercurrent | Indicates whether there is an overcurrent condition on the channel. |
| SensorPowerTypes | Indicates the types of power supplied to the sensor supported by this channel. |
| SensorPowerVoltageRangeValues | Indicates pairs of sensor power voltage ranges supported by this channel. Each pair consists of the low value followed by the high value. |
| TedsBitStream | Indicates the TEDS binary bitstream without checksums. |
| TedsManufacturerID | Indicates the manufacturer ID of the sensor. |
| TedsModelNumber | Indicates the model number of the sensor. |
| TedsSerialNumber | Indicates the serial number of the sensor. |
| TedsTemplateIDs | Indicates the IDs of the templates in the bitstream in TedsBitStream. |
| TedsVersionLetter | Indicates the version letter of the sensor. |
| TedsVersionNumber | Indicates the version number of the sensor. |

#### Methods

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| ClearTeds() | Removes TEDS information from the physical channel you specify. |
| ConfigureTeds() | Associates TEDS information with the physical channel you specify, using a TEDS sensor connected to the physical channel. |
| ConfigureTeds(string) | Associates TEDS information with the physical channel you specify. |
| Dispose() | Releases all resources used by PhysicalChannel. |
| ToString() | Returns a string representation of the object. |
| WriteTedsData(string, BasicTedsDataOption) | Write TEDS data from a virtual TEDS file to a sensor on the physical channel you specify. |
| WriteTedsData(byte[], BasicTedsDataOption) | Write TEDS data from a Byte array to a sensor on the physical channel you specify. |
| Dispose(bool) | Releases the managed and unmanaged resources used by PhysicalChannel or optionally releases only the unmanaged resources. |

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 02496: ForwardCoefficients

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-polynomialscale-forwardcoefficients.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-polynomialscale-forwardcoefficients.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies an array of coefficients for the polynomial that converts pre-scaled values to scaled values. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index three of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9x^3. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxp

### ForwardCoefficients

Specifies an array of coefficients for the polynomial that converts pre-scaled values to scaled values. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index three of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9x^3.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public double[] ForwardCoefficients { get; set; }

#### Remarks

This property returns a copy of the actual array. Avoid calling this property within a for loop because it creates a copy for each iteration of the loop. Avoid using an indexer to set a member of the array because the indexer returns a copy of the object and has no effect on the actual object.

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

PolynomialScale Class

### PolynomialScale(string, double[], double[])

Creates a new instance of the [PolynomialScale](nationalinstruments-daqmx-polynomialscale.html) class with the specified forward and reverse coefficients.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public PolynomialScale(string name, double[] forwardCoefficients, double[] reverseCoefficients)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| name | string | The name of the custom scale for later use, such as when you create a virtual channel. |
| forwardCoefficients | double[] | The array of the forward coefficients of the polynomial. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index three of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9x3. |
| reverseCoefficients | double[] | The array of the reverse coefficients of the polynomial. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index three of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9y3. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

## TOPIC 02498: PolynomialScale(string, PolynomialDirection, double[], double, double, int, int)

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- source_path: `nationalinstruments-daqmx-polynomialscale-polynomialscale__string-polynomialdirection-double_arr1-double-double-int-int.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/nationalinstruments-daqmx-polynomialscale-polynomialscale__string-polynomialdirection-double_arr1-double-double-int-int.html
- document_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Creates a new instance of the PolynomialScale class with the specified forward or reverse coefficients and automatically computes the other set of coefficients. SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic PolynomialScale(string name, PolynomialDirection direction, double[] coefficients, double

### PolynomialScale(string, PolynomialDirection, double[], double, double, int, int)

Creates a new instance of the [PolynomialScale](nationalinstruments-daqmx-polynomialscale.html) class with the specified forward or reverse coefficients and automatically computes the other set of coefficients.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public PolynomialScale(string name, PolynomialDirection direction, double[] coefficients, double rangeMinimum, double rangeMaximum, int numberOfPointsInFit, int orderOfFit)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| name | string | The name of the custom scale for later use, such as when you create a virtual channel. |
| direction | PolynomialDirection | The conversion direction of the specified polynomial. The opposite polynomial is computed by the PolynomialScale. |
| coefficients | double[] | The array of coefficients of a polynomial. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index three of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9x3. This polynomial is used as either the forward or reverse polynomial depending on the direction specified. |
| rangeMinimum | double | The minimum of the range over which the polynomial specified is valid or of interest. |
| rangeMaximum | double | The maximum of the range over which the polynomial specified is valid or of interest. |
| numberOfPointsInFit | int | The number of points to evaluate for computing the polynomial of the opposite direction. |
| orderOfFit | int | The order of polynomial to compute for the opposite polynomial to the one provided. Specify -1 to use the same order as the forward polynomial. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

PolynomialScale Class

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref path=nationalinstruments-daqmx-polynomialscale-polynomialscale__string-polynomialdirection-double_arr1-double-double.html language=enus -->

- bundle_id: `ni-daqmx-net-framework-api-ref`

SyntaxNamespace: NationalInstruments.DAQmxpublic

### PolynomialScale(string, PolynomialDirection, double[], double, double)

Creates a new instance of the [PolynomialScale](nationalinstruments-daqmx-polynomialscale.html) class with the specified forward or reverse coefficients and automatically computes the other set of coefficients with the same order as the provided coefficients, using 1000 points in the specified range.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public PolynomialScale(string name, PolynomialDirection direction, double[] coefficients, double rangeMinimum, double rangeMaximum)

#### Parameters

| Name | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| name | string | The name of the custom scale for later use, such as when you create a virtual channel. |
| direction | PolynomialDirection | The conversion direction of the specified polynomial. The opposite polynomial is computed by the PolynomialScale. |
| coefficients | double[] | The array of coefficients of a polynomial. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index three of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9x3. This polynomial is used as either the forward or reverse polynomial depending on the direction specified. |
| rangeMinimum | double | The minimum of the range over which the polynomial specified is valid or of interest. |
| rangeMaximum | double | The maximum of the range over which the polynomial specified is valid or of interest. |

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |

Parent topic:

### ReverseCoefficients

Specifies an array of coefficients for the polynomial that converts scaled values to pre-scaled values. Each element of the array corresponds to a term of the equation. For example, if index three of the array is 9, the fourth term of the equation is 9y^3.

#### Syntax

**Namespace:**[NationalInstruments.DAQmx](nationalinstruments-daqmx.html)

public double[] ReverseCoefficients { get; set; }

#### Remarks

This property returns a copy of the actual array. Avoid calling this property within a for loop because it creates a copy for each iteration of the loop. Avoid using an indexer to set a member of the array because the indexer returns a copy of the object and has no effect on the actual object.

#### Exceptions

| Type | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NationalInstruments.DAQmx.DaqException | The NI-DAQmx driver returned an error. |
